A full house gives you twenty-five points.\r\n\r\nA Yatzy is five of a kind and gives you fifty points for the first Yatzy and one hundred points for each additional Yatzy in the same game column.\r\n\r\nThe second Yatzy must be put in the upper score box for the number you rolled if available (i.e. five 5‚Äôs would score twenty-five in the fives box and an additional one hundred points in the Yatzy bonus).\r\n\r\nIf the upper score box for the number you rolled is filled, you may place the score in any available box in the bottom section or place a zero in one of the boxes in the upper section.\r\n\r\nMost players choose to put all Yatzys in the same game column and zero out the others.
